<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="English">English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=hello&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: English">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="NavFrame" style="background-color:#FFB90F;">
<div class="NavHead" style="background:#FFFFbf;">English phrasebook</div>
<div class="NavContent">
<table style="background-color:#FFFFbf; width:100%; margin: auto; text-align:center">

<tbody><tr>
<td style="text-align:left;"><a href="/wiki/File:Open_book_01.svg" class="image"><img alt="Open book 01.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/Open_book_01.svg/40px-Open_book_01.svg.png" decoding="async" width="40" height="40" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/Open_book_01.svg/60px-Open_book_01.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f3/Open_book_01.svg/80px-Open_book_01.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="360" data-file-height="360" /></a>
</td>
<td>This entry is part of the <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:Phrasebook" title="Wiktionary:Phrasebook">phrasebook</a> project, which presents <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:Criteria_for_inclusion" title="Wiktionary:Criteria for inclusion">criteria for inclusion</a> based on utility, simplicity and commonality.<div>For other English entries on this topic, see <b><a href="/wiki/Category:English_phrasebook/Greetings" title="Category:English phrasebook/Greetings">Greetings</a></b>.</div>
</td></tr></tbody></table></div></div>
<div class="was-wotd floatright" style="padding-right: 1em"><span title="This was a Wiktionary Word of the Day"><small><i><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:Word_of_the_day/Archive/2007/November#19" title="Wiktionary:Word of the day/Archive/2007/November">WOTD –&#32;19 November 2007</a></i></small></span></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=hello&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Alternative forms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/hallo#English" title="hallo">hallo</a></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">UK old style</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/hilloa#English" title="hilloa">hilloa</a></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/hullo#English" title="hullo">hullo</a></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">UK</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=hello&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><i>Hello</i> (first attested in 1826), from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/holla#English" title="holla">holla</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/hollo#English" title="hollo">hollo</a></i> (attested 1588). This variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/hallo#English" title="hallo">hallo</a></i> is often credited to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thomas_Edison" class="extiw" title="w:Thomas Edison">Thomas Edison</a> as a coinage for telephone use, but its appearance in print predates the invention of the telephone by several decades.
</p><p>Ultimately from a variant of Old English <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/eala#Old_English" title="eala">ēalā</a></i>, such as <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang"><a href="/wiki/hela#Old_English" title="hela">hēlā</a></i>, which was used colloquially at the time similarly to how <i>hey</i> and <i>hi</i> are used nowadays. Thus, equivalent to a compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/hey#English" title="hey">hey</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/lo#English" title="lo">lo</a></i>. Used when drawing attention to yourself.
</p><p>Possibly influenced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx"><a href="/wiki/halo#Old_Saxon" title="halo">halo!</a></i>, imperative of <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx"><a href="/wiki/halon#Old_Saxon" title="halon">halōn</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to call, fetch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, used in hailing a ferryman, akin to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href="/wiki/hala#Old_High_German" title="hala">hala</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href="/wiki/hola#Old_High_German" title="hola">hola!</a></i>, imperative forms of <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href="/wiki/halon#Old_High_German" title="halon">halōn</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href="/wiki/holon#Old_High_German" title="holon">holōn</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to fetch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/hallo#English" title="hallo">hallo</a></span>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=hello&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/British_English" class="extiw" title="w:British English">UK</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/həˈləʊ/</span>, <span class="IPA">/hɛˈləʊ/</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_English" class="extiw" title="w:American English">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">enPR</a>: <span class="AHD enPR">hĕ-lō'</span>, <span class="AHD enPR">hə-lō'</span>, <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>:&#32;<span class="IPA">/hɛˈloʊ/</span>, <span class="IPA">/həˈloʊ/</span>, <span class="IPA">/ˈhɛloʊ/</span></li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=hello&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Interjection">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">hello</strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">A <a href="/wiki/greeting#English" title="greeting">greeting</a> (<a href="/wiki/salutation#English" title="salutation">salutation</a>) said when <a href="/wiki/meet#English" title="meet">meeting</a> someone or <a href="/wiki/acknowledge#English" title="acknowledge">acknowledging</a> someone’s <a href="/wiki/arrival#English" title="arrival">arrival</a> or <a href="/wiki/presence#English" title="presence">presence</a>.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><b>Hello</b>, everyone.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">A greeting used when <a href="/wiki/answer#English" title="answer">answering</a> the <a href="/wiki/telephone#English" title="telephone">telephone</a>.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><b>Hello</b>? How may I help you?</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>2016</b>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20170918070146/https://learningenglish.voanews.com/a/lets-learn-english-lesson-3-i-am-here/3126527.html">VOA Learning English</a> (public domain)
<dl><dd><b>Hello</b>. This is Marsha. - Yes, Marsha.
<dl><dd><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r50165410"/><table class="audiotable" style="vertical-align: bottom; display:inline-block; list-style:none;line-height: 1em; border-collapse:collapse;"><tbody><tr><td class="unicode audiolink" style="padding-right:5px; padding-left: 0;">Audio (US)</td><td class="audiofile"><div class="mediaContainer" style="width:175px"><audio id="mwe_player_11" controls="" preload="none" style="width:175px" class="kskin" data-durationhint="3.8949659863946" data-startoffset="0" data-mwtitle="Hello._This_is_Marsha._-_Yes,_Marsha.ogg" data-mwprovider="wikimediacommons"><source src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/transcoded/0/0d/Hello._This_is_Marsha._-_Yes%2C_Marsha.ogg/Hello._This_is_Marsha._-_Yes%2C_Marsha.ogg.mp3" type="audio/mpeg" data-title="MP3" data-shorttitle="MP3" data-transcodekey="mp3" data-width="0" data-height="0" data-bandwidth="91880" /><source src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/0/0d/Hello._This_is_Marsha._-_Yes%2C_Marsha.ogg" type="audio/ogg; codecs=&quot;vorbis&quot;" data-title="Original Ogg file (113 kbps)" data-shorttitle="Ogg source" data-width="0" data-height="0" data-bandwidth="112742" /></audio></div></td><td class="audiometa" style="font-size: 80%;">(<a href="/wiki/File:Hello._This_is_Marsha._-_Yes,_Marsha.ogg" title="File:Hello. This is Marsha. - Yes, Marsha.ogg">file</a>)</td></tr></tbody></table></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">A call for <a href="/wiki/response#English" title="response">response</a> if it is not clear if anyone is present or listening, or if a telephone conversation may have been <a href="/wiki/disconnect#English" title="disconnect">disconnected</a>.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><b>Hello</b>? Is anyone there?</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1913</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joseph_C._Lincoln" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Joseph C. Lincoln">Joseph C. Lincoln</a>,  chapter 7, in  <cite><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://openlibrary.org/works/OL5535161W">Mr. Pratt's Patients</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">I made a speaking trumpet of my hands and commenced to whoop “Ahoy!” and “<b>Hello!</b>” at the top of my lungs. <span class="q-hellip-sp">&#32;</span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b">&#32;</span> The Colonel woke up, and, after asking what in brimstone was the matter, opened his mouth and roared “Hi!” and “<b>Hello!</b>” like the bull of Bashan.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#colloquial" title="Appendix:Glossary">colloquial</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Used <a href="/wiki/sarcastic#English" title="sarcastic">sarcastically</a> to imply that the person addressed or referred to has done something the speaker or writer considers to be <a href="/wiki/foolish#English" title="foolish">foolish</a>.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">You just tried to start your car with your cell phone. <b>Hello</b>?</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly&#32;<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">An expression of <a href="/wiki/puzzlement#English" title="puzzlement">puzzlement</a> or <a href="/wiki/discovery#English" title="discovery">discovery</a>.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en"><b>Hello</b>! What’s going on here?</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=hello&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Usage notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<ul><li>The greeting <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/hello#English" title="hello">hello</a></i> is among the most universal and neutral in use. It may be heard in nearly all social situations and nearly all walks of life and is unlikely to offend.</li></ul>

<ul><li><span class="see-cites">For quotations using this term, see <a href="/wiki/Citations:hello#English" title="Citations:hello">Citations:hello</a>.</span></li></ul>

<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">greeting</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="see-cites"><i>See</i> <a href="/wiki/Thesaurus:hello#English" title="Thesaurus:hello">Thesaurus:hello</a></span>

<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">US, informal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/hallo" title="hallo">hallo</a>, <a href="/wiki/hey" title="hey">hey</a>, <a href="/wiki/hi" title="hi">hi</a>, <a href="/wiki/howdy" title="howdy">howdy</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">Ireland, informal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/how%27s_it_going" title="how&#39;s it going">how's it going</a>, <a href="/wiki/hey" title="hey">hey</a>, <a href="/wiki/hi" title="hi">hi</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">South Africa, informal</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/howzit" title="howzit">howzit</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/wassup" title="wassup">wassup</a>, <a href="/wiki/what%27s_up" title="what&#39;s up">what's up</a>, <a href="/wiki/yo" title="yo">yo</a>, <a href="/wiki/sup" title="sup">sup</a>, <a href="/wiki/what%27s_good" title="what&#39;s good">what's good</a></li></ul></li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=hello&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">hello</strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/hellos#English" title="hellos">hellos</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/helloes#English" title="helloes">helloes</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>"<a href="/wiki/hello#Interjection" title="hello">Hello</a>!" or an equivalent greeting.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2007</b> April 29,  Stephanie Rosenbloom,  “A Beautiful Day in the Neighborhood”, in  <cite>New York Times</cite>&#8206;<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2007/04/29/fashion/29condo.html">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">In many new buildings, though, neighbors are venturing beyond tight-lipped <b>hellos</b> at the mailbox.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=hello&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Verb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">hello</strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3&#124;s&#124;pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/hellos#English" title="hellos">hellos</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres&#124;ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/helloing#English" title="helloing">helloing</a></b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past&#124;and&#124;past&#124;ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/helloed#English" title="helloed">helloed</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#transitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">transitive</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To <a href="/wiki/greet" title="greet">greet</a> with "hello".
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2013</b>,  Ivan Doig,  <cite>English Creek</cite>, page 139:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">I had to traipse around somewhat, <b>helloing</b> people and being <b>helloed</b>, before I spotted my mother and my father, sharing shade and a spread blanket with Pete and Marie Reese and Toussaint Rennie near the back of the park.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=hello&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=hello&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="ff">hello</strong>&#32;<i><a href="/wiki/ngo#Fula" title="ngo">ngo</a></i>&#32;(<i>plural</i> <b><a href="/w/index.php?title=hellooji&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="hellooji (page does not exist)">hellooji</a></b>&#32;<i><a href="/wiki/%C9%97i#Fula" title="ɗi">ɗi</a></i>)
</p>
<ol><li>a <a href="/wiki/page" title="page">page</a></li>
<li>one side of a <a href="/wiki/wall" title="wall">wall</a>, a wall</li>
<li>a <a href="/wiki/slap" title="slap">slap</a> in the face</li></ol>
